                win.uet("be", "LoadFonts", { wb: 1 });
                win.uex("ld", "LoadFonts", { wb: 1 });
            }
        }).catch(function() {
            if (win.ue) {
                win.ue.count("font-loaded", 0);
            }
        });
    } else {
        if (win.ue) {
            win.ue.count("font-load-not-attempted", 1);
        }
    }
